2  #define GTEST_INCLUDE_GTEST_INTERNAL_GTEST_TYPE_UTIL_H_
3  #include "gtest/internal/gtest-port.h"
4  # if GTEST_HAS_CXXABI_H_
5  #  include <cxxabi.h>
6  # elif defined(__HP_aCC)
7  #  include <acxx_demangle.h>

9  namespace testing {
10  namespace internal {
11  template <typename T>
12  std::string GetTypeName() {
13  # if GTEST_HAS_RTTI
14    const char* const name = typeid(T).name();
15  #  if GTEST_HAS_CXXABI_H_ || defined(__HP_aCC)
16    int status = 0;
17  #   if GTEST_HAS_CXXABI_H_
18    using abi::__cxa_demangle;
19  #   endif  
20    char* const readable_name = __cxa_demangle(name, 0, 0, &status);
21    const std::string name_str(status == 0 ? readable_name : name);
22    free(readable_name);
23    return name_str;
24  #  else
25    return name;
26  #  endif  
27  # else
28    return "<type>";
29  # endif  
30  }

11  template <typename T>
12  std::string GetTypeName() {
13  # if GTEST_HAS_RTTI
14    const char* const name = typeid(T).name();
15  #  if GTEST_HAS_CXXABI_H_ || defined(__HP_aCC)
16    int status = 0;
17  #   if GTEST_HAS_CXXABI_H_
18    using abi::__cxa_demangle;
19  #   endif  
20    char* const readable_name = __cxa_demangle(name, 0, 0, &status);
21    const std::string name_str(status == 0 ? readable_name : name);
22    free(readable_name);
23    return name_str;
24  #  else
25    return name;
26  #  endif  
27  # else
28    return "<type>";
29  # endif  
30  }
